  function setCartData(cartData, adapter) {
    adapter.Cart.clear();

    cartData.cart.forEach(cartItem => {
      adapter.Cart.add(cartItem.sku, {quantity: cartItem.quantity, price: cartItem.price, name: cartItem.name});
    });

		<li>$100 Loyalty Reward Gift Card (subscriptions $176 per month and over) each time you successfully complete 4 consecutive RPS deliveries. Gift cards can be redeemed on future orders.</li>

<script>
// Get the modal
var modal = document.getElementById("myModal");

// Get the button that opens the modal
var btn = document.getElementById("mypopupBtn1");

// Get the <span> element that closes the modal
var span = document.getElementsByClassName("close")[0];
window.onload = function () {
//2021-11-11 added btn.onclick inside window.onload = function () {
// When the user clicks the button, open the modal 
	if(btn){
		btn.onclick = function() {
		  modal.style.display = "block";
		  //jQuery(modal).fadeIn(300);
		}
	}
}

// When the user clicks on <span> (x), close the modal
span.onclick = function() {
  modal.style.display = "none";
  //jQuery(modal).fadeOut(300);
}

// When the user clicks anywhere outside of the modal, close it
window.onclick = function(event) {
  if (event.target == modal) {
    modal.style.display = "none";
  }
